msg:Yuelai Hotel is perfect, low-key and luxurious, and very comfortable to stay.
I took my parents out, my mother was in a wheelchair, and the hotel had perfect barrier-free facilities. The picture shows that the staff helped us upgrade the room type to a suite.
The hotel is in a great location. Just across the road from the beach, the hotel can also send a car to the door for free.
I had lunch and dinner in the hotel restaurant. The price was not expensive, the taste was good, and the set meal was very cost-effective. In short, it was delicious and not expensive.
The suite had a large balcony and a large bathtub. Taking a bath and overlooking the sea was really the best way to go on vacation.
The staff was very enthusiastic. I split my nails and helped me get a band-aid.
The hotel has complete facilities, the gym is not small, and the laundry room can be self-service or handed over to the staff for free laundry and drying. This is really helpful.
I also gave a souvenir when I checked out. If I have the opportunity to travel to Xiamen again, I will definitely stay here again.

It is just across the road from the beach. On the opposite side, you can see the big and small Kinmen Islands. Next to it is the big Chinese characters "One country, two systems, unifying China". The scenery is very beautiful Pleasant, the sand on the beach is very fine, there are few people, away from the hustle and bustle of other popular areas. Special mention should be made of the hotel's services. There are free shuttle buses in the park to take guests to and from the main building, the gate and various villa buildings, and they are on call. The most surprising thing is that the top-floor presidential suite was upgraded for free on the night of check-in. The room is super large , The facilities are complete, clean and hygienic, you can face the sea directly when you open the window, and enjoy the sea breeze. I feel that it is a waste of such a good room without my family on a business trip; the front desk also recommended the hotel's current 1 yuan breakfast service, breakfast Very rich and definitely worth the money. My favorite is the freshly cooked seafood noodles at the breakfast stall (sixties, oysters, fresh shrimp, pork liver, and shredded lean pork cooked together); when leaving, the waiter also thoughtfully sent a box of sun rock stuffing Cake souvenirs, the service is really great. I will definitely stay here next time I come to Xiamen.
